- ~~**Phase F.10.1: `gjsify flatpak sync-flathub` ŌĆö automated Flathub tracking-repo updates**~~Ō£ō ŌĆö Flathub publishes each app from a separate `flathub/<app-id>` tracking-repo whose manifest pins the upstream `tag` + `commit` SHA. Before this command, every release required hand-editing that pin in a checkout, branching, committing, pushing, and opening a PR ŌĆö error-prone, easy to skip, drifts between `gjsify.flatpak` config and the published Flathub-manifest. New `gjsify flatpak sync-flathub` (`packages/infra/cli/src/commands/flatpak/sync-flathub.ts`, ~340 LoC) automates the loop: resolves `appId` from `gjsify.flatpak.appId`, `flathubRepo` from new optional `gjsify.flatpak.flathubRepo` field (default `flathub/<appId>`), `--version` from `git describe --tags --abbrev=0` in cwd, `--commit` from `git rev-list -n 1 <tag>`. Clones (or fetches + hard-resets) the tracking-repo into `$XDG_CACHE_HOME/gjsify/flathub-sync/<repo>/`, auto-detects the default branch via `git remote show origin` (handles `master` vs `main`), then surgically edits `modules[0].sources[<i>]` (`.tag` + `.commit`, injects an `x-checker-data` block if missing so Flathub's auto-update bot can pick up future releases). JSON preserved with the source file's original indent ŌĆö Flathub convention is 2-space (matches Phase G.2's `flatpak init` default) but the indent detector keeps anything else verbatim. Then branches to `update-to-<version>`, commits with message `Update to <version>`, pushes with `--force-with-lease`, and opens a PR via `gh pr create --repo <flathub-repo> --head <branch> --title "Update to <version>"`. Flags: `--version`, `--app-id`, `--flathub-repo`, `--commit`, `--branch`, `--source-index` (for manifests with multiple `git` sources), `--no-pr` (skip push + gh), `--dry-run`, `--verbose`. Idempotent ŌĆö re-running with the same version is detected (`manifest already at <version> ŌĆö nothing to do`) and short-circuits without push or PR. ENOENT on `git` / `gh` produces distro-specific install hints. New e2e suite `tests/e2e/flatpak-sync/` (4 tests, ~1.3s): dry-run resolution + commit-only + open-PR + idempotent no-op. Test rig stubs `git` (clone copies a fixture manifest into the simulated clone-dir; other subcommands no-op success) and `gh` (records invocations); CLI runs from the locally built `lib/index.js` so the suite is independent of the workspace-pack machinery. Wired into `test:e2e` aggregator. New `flathubRepo` field on `ConfigDataFlatpak`. Docs in `website/src/content/docs/cli-reference.md`. Companion follow-up: `gjsify flatpak diff` (F.10.2) + `gjsify flatpak release` (F.10.3, chains init+check+tag+sync-flathub).

- ~~**`Buffer.from(SharedBuffer)` + `SharedBuffer.toBuffer()` ŌĆö ergonomic Buffer interop for `@gjsify/sab-native`**~~Ō£ō ŌĆö Closes the "feels like Node" gap for SharedBuffer consumers: `Buffer.from(sb)` now works directly without a manual `Buffer.from(sb.readBytes(0, sb.byteLength))` ceremony. Implementation lives across two packages without creating a dep cycle. `@gjsify/sab-native` gains `SharedBuffer.viewBytes(offset, length)` (stable duck-type entry ŌĆö currently an alias for `readBytes()`) and `SharedBuffer.toBuffer<T = Uint8Array>(offset?, length?)` (resolves `globalThis.Buffer` lazily; generic-typed to avoid an import dep on `@gjsify/buffer`). `@gjsify/buffer` extends `Buffer.from` with a structural overload that recognises any object with `viewBytes(o, l): Uint8Array` + `byteLength: number` + `constructor.name === 'SharedBuffer'` ŌĆö duck-typing keeps `@gjsify/buffer` at the bottom of the dep tree. **Honest semantics:** in current GJS the result is a fresh memcpy, not a true zero-copy view ŌĆö `byteArray.fromGBytes` (refs/gjs/gjs/byteArray.cpp::from_gbytes_func) actively copies via `JS::NewArrayBuffer`. The structural contract (`viewBytes` shape) is forward-compatible with a future C-level `JS::NewExternalArrayBuffer` shim that would flip the semantics to truly-zero-copy without API change. Tracked as a new entry under "Upstream GJS Patch Candidates". Tests: 326/326 buffer GJS + 317/317 buffer Node + 58/58 sab-native GJS (4 new viewBytes/toBuffer tests + 5 new Buffer.from(sharedBufferLike) tests). worker_threads + worker-stress remain green (275/270/1035/1169).

- ~~**Phase G.2: `flatpak init` 2-space JSON + optional biome-aware post-format**~~Ō£ō ŌĆö Two coupled improvements stacked on G.1. (1) `flatpak init` now writes the manifest with 2-space indentation (was 4-space), matching the Flathub-tracking-repo convention (e.g. `flathub/eu.jumplink.Learn6502/eu.jumplink.Learn6502.json` is 2-space) AND biome's + prettier's defaults. Eliminates the prettier-fix step from Learn6502#96. (2) New `--format` flag (default `true`): when `@biomejs/biome` is in `package.json#devDependencies` (detected via `hasBiomeDevDep()`), init runs `biome format --write` on the four generated outputs (manifest + .metainfo.xml.in + .desktop.in + flathub.json) so they harmonise with the project's biome.json style. `--no-format` skips. When biome is declared but the binary isn't actually installed (e.g. `gjsify install` not yet run), the post-format step degrades to a warning rather than failing. e2e suite extended 14 ŌåÆ 17 tests covering: 2-space output assertion, biome-aware post-format with biome.json, --no-format skip. Backwards compatible ŌĆö projects without biome get the bare 2-space output (still better than 4-space because 2-space is the broader convention).

- ~~**Phase G.1: `gjsify format` / `gjsify lint` / `gjsify fix` + recommended biome.json defaults**~~Ō£ō ŌĆö Three new CLI commands wrapping Biome's native binary. `gjsify` resolves `node_modules/@biomejs/cli-<platform>-<arch>/biome` directly (skipping the Node-launcher in `@biomejs/biome/bin/biome`) and spawns it via `spawn(bin, args, { stdio: 'inherit' })`. Same Node-free pattern as `gjsify gettext` (ŌåÆ msgfmt), `gjsify gresource` (ŌåÆ glib-compile-resources), `gjsify gsettings` (ŌåÆ glib-compile-schemas). Three commands: `format` (whitespace-only, `--write`/`--check`), `lint` (default report, `--write` for safe-fixes), `fix` (biome's `check --write` ŌĆö format + safe-lint-fix + organize-imports in one pass; deliberately distinct name from `gjsify check` which verifies system deps). New `findBiomeBin(cwd)` util in `utils/biome-resolve.ts` does platform/arch detection (`process.platform`, `process.arch`), musl-detection (probes `/lib/ld-musl-*`), and walks `cwd ŌåÆ workspace-root ŌåÆ parent dirs` to find the right `@biomejs/cli-<platform>-<arch>` package. `--init` writes a recommended `biome.json` template (`packages/infra/cli/src/templates/biome.json.tmpl`, inlined via static-read-inliner) tuned for GJS projects: JS/TS 4-space indent (matches GJS-codebase + GNOME Shell convention), JSON+CSS 2-space (Flathub manifest + GTK4-CSS convention), single quotes, semicolons, line width 120, Biome's `recommended: true` linter + 4 GJS-specific opt-outs (`noNonNullAssertion: off` for `@girs/*` API patterns, `noExplicitAny: warn` for cross-runtime cast chains, `noConsole: off` for GJS logging convention, `useImportType: warn` non-blocking). `files.includes` excludes `dist`/`lib`/`refs`/build dirs/Flatpak artifacts/compiled `.metainfo.xml`. Workspace-aware: single `biome.json` at workspace root applies to all sub-workspaces (Biome v2 globbing handles this natively); `findBiomeConfig(cwd)` walks up. Standalone projects use same shape at project root. `ConfigData.format?: { configPath? }` for explicit override. New e2e suite `tests/e2e/biome/` (8 tests, ~61s): `--init` template content verification, `--init` skip-without-`--force`, `format --write` round-trip, `format --check` non-zero on drift, workspace-root resolution from sub-workspace, ENOENT install hint, `lint` reports + `--write` safe-fix (`useConst`), `fix` combined pass. Backwards compatible ŌĆö no impact on existing commands.

- ~~**`examples/node/cli-sab-parallel-hash` ŌĆö 4-worker SHA-256 showcase (Message-Channel Unification Step 3, PR-C)**~~Ō£ō ŌĆö New private example sibling to `cli-worker-pool/`, lifts the 4-worker SHA-256 pattern from `tests/integration/worker-stress/src/sab-native-parallel-hash.gjs.spec.ts` into a polished CLI demo of `@gjsify/sab-native` ├Ś `@gjsify/worker_threads`. Splits a deterministic 4 MiB payload into four 1 MiB slices, spawns 4 cross-process workers via `node:worker_threads`, each hashes its slice with `GLib.Checksum.SHA256` and writes the 32-byte digest back into the shared region via the same memfd. Parent polls the per-worker barrier (`atomics.load32`) on a 2 ms `setTimeout` cadence to stay responsive, then XOR-folds the four digests and verifies the result against a single-threaded reference computed via `node:crypto`. Demonstrates `SharedBuffer.create`, `sb.setUint8` / `sb.readBytes`, `atomics.store32` / `atomics.load32`, `Worker.postMessage(value, [sb])` (SCM_RIGHTS over inherited fd 3), and `workerData: { sb }` spawn-time hand-off. Verified: per-worker MiB/s + total wall time + digest match. Node target prints a friendly note pointing back to GJS (sab-native is GJS-only). Examples count: 52 ŌåÆ 53.

- ~~**worker_threads MessagePort via Composition on `@gjsify/message-channel` (Message-Channel Unification Step 3, PR-B)**~~Ō£ō ŌĆö Refactors `packages/node/worker_threads/src/message-port.ts` to compose a private `_inner: SharedMessagePort` from `@gjsify/message-channel` while still `extends EventEmitter` (required by `@types/node`'s declaration). Single source of truth for the W3C surface ŌĆö `addEventListener('message')` / `addEventListener('messageerror')` / `onmessage` IDL setter / `start()` / `close()` / queue + microtask dispatch ŌĆö all live in the shared base. The wrapper owns transferList semantics (ArrayBuffer / MessagePort / SharedBuffer pass-through) and the EventEmitter side (`port.on('message')` auto-starts, mirrors the inner's started-state, replays the queue on start). `addEventListener('message')` does NOT auto-start (matches Node + W3C HTML ┬¦9.4.4) ŌĆö implemented by bypassing the shared MP's developer-friendly auto-start override and calling `EventTarget.prototype.addEventListener` on the inner directly. `addEventListener('close', ...)` routes to EventEmitter because `'close'` is Node-only and not a W3C MessagePort event. Trade-off (acceptable per plan): `port instanceof worker_threadsMP === true` but `port instanceof sharedMP === false`. All counts unchanged: **275/275 GJS unit + 270/270 Node unit + 1035/1035 GJS integration + 1169/1169 Node integration**, all green. New `@gjsify/message-channel` workspace dep added. `port._inner` is accessible for introspection.

- ~~**Phase F.9.7: `gjsify.flatpak.name` config field ŌĆö display-name override**~~Ō£ō ŌĆö One-field fix surfaced while migrating easy6502 (the first real-world consumer of F.9.6's full AppStream surface). `gjsify flatpak init` was deriving the MetaInfo `<name>` + .desktop `Name=` from a `friendlyName(pkgName, appId)` helper. - ~~**`@gjsify/sab-native` + `@gjsify/worker_threads` cross-process SharedBuffer (Workstream C close)**~~Ō£ō ŌĆö Three-PR sprint closing the Workstream C follow-up Open TODO. **PR1 (Phase 0):** new `@gjsify/sab-native` package ŌĆö Vala/C bridge over Linux libc primitives (memfd_create + mmap(MAP_SHARED) for `SharedBuffer`; SOCK_SEQPACKET socketpair + SCM_RIGHTS for `FdChannel`; SEQ_CST `__atomic_*` + `syscall(SYS_futex, FUTEX_{WAIT,WAKE})` for cross-process atomics ŌĆö the non-PRIVATE flag is load-bearing because per-Worker virtual addresses differ but the underlying memfd pages are the same). 18 GJS specs green including a real cross-process round-trip via `Gio.SubprocessLauncher.take_fd(fd, 3)`. Wire protocol is byte-order-explicit LE on every accessor so a buffer written on x86_64 reads identically on s390x. Prebuilds for linux-{x86_64, aarch64, ppc64, s390x, riscv64} via the existing prebuilds.yml workflow (pure libc, no external library deps, so no rustup / submodule init overhead). **PR2 (Phase 1):** `@gjsify/worker_threads` ├Ś `@gjsify/sab-native` integration. `Worker.postMessage(value, [sab])` and `workerData: { sab }` now route SharedBuffer instances across the subprocess-Worker boundary. Parent spawns each Worker with a SOCK_SEQPACKET socketpair (`FdChannel.makePair()`), passes the child end as inherited fd 3 via `Gio.SubprocessLauncher.take_fd`, and per-message walks the value tree for SharedBuffer instances, SCM_RIGHTS-sends each fd tagged with a sequence counter, then writes a JSON line with `{__sab: tag, size: N}` placeholders. The bootstrap counts placeholders per inbound message and synchronously drains exactly that many fds from fd 3 ŌĆö kernel buffering guarantees the fds are ready since the parent always writes them before the stdin line ŌĆö then rebuilds each placeholder via `SharedBuffer.fromFd(fd, size)`. In-process MessagePort transferList accepts SharedBuffer too (no fd-passing needed ŌĆö same JS heap). `structured-clone.ts` extended with a SharedBuffer pass-through branch (same shape as the SharedArrayBuffer branch ŌĆö constructor-name probe so utils stays independent of sab-native in the dep graph). 4 new worker_threads GJS unit tests + 1 new worker-stress integration test (4 workers ├Ś SHA-256 over 1 MiB SharedBuffer; XOR-folded digest matches in-process reference). **PR3 (Phase 2):** hardening + docs. 8-worker ├Ś 10,000 fetch_add stress test (80,000 increments observed exactly ŌĆö no lost updates under multi-process SEQ_CST contention, no fd leak across 8 concurrent spawn/terminate cycles). AGENTS.md worker_threads row updated; STATUS.md Open TODO renamed from "SharedArrayBuffer cross-process sharing" to "SharedArrayBuffer constructor opt-in (Mozilla pref)" ŌĆö what's left is just the upstream-GJS SAB-constructor pref. Counts: 275/275 GJS unit + 1035/1035 GJS integration + 270/270 Node unit + 1169/1169 Node integration.

- ~~**Phase F.8: `gjsify uninstall -g <pkg>`**~~Ō£ō ŌĆö Symmetric inverse of `gjsify install -g`. `commands/uninstall.ts` (~120 LoC) removes the installed package tree from `~/.local/share/gjsify/global/node_modules/<pkg>/` plus any bin shims under `~/.local/bin/` whose POSIX `sh` launcher exec's into the removed tree. Shim discovery parses the launcher script (`exec '<path>'` or `exec gjs -m '<path>'`) and matches the absolute path ŌĆö non-gjsify-shim files in the same bin dir are skipped silently. Flags: `--global`/`-g` (required; project-local uninstall is a separate workstream that needs lockfile rewrites), `--dry-run` (print "would remove" without touching FS), `--verbose`. Exits non-zero when nothing was removed. New e2e suite `tests/e2e/uninstall-global/` (4 tests, ~2.5s): full installŌåÆuninstall round-trip, `--dry-run` leaves FS untouched, not-installed package exits non-zero, missing `--global` is a clear error. Wired into `test:e2e` aggregator. Docs in `website/src/content/docs/cli-reference.md`.

- ~~**Phase F.5: ts-for-gir CI fully Node-free via install.mjs**~~Ō£ō ŌĆö Migration of ts-for-gir's four CI workflows (`ci.yml` + `release-{app,docs,types}.yml`) from `npm install -g @gjsify/cli@^0.4.14` to the production `curl -fsSL .../install.mjs | gjs -m -` bootstrap. Runner moved from `ubuntu-latest` to `ubuntu-latest` with a `fedora:43` container ŌĆö required because ubuntu-latest ships gjs 1.80 (below install.mjs's 1.86 minimum); Fedora 43 ships gjs 1.86 / SM 140, matching gjsify's own CI host setup. apt ŌåÆ dnf package mapping for the GTK/GNOME -devel set in `build-validate`. `actions/setup-node` replaced with a tiny inline `~/.npmrc` writer for `release-app.yml`'s npm auth (publish still flows through `gjsify publish` from Phase E, which honors `NPM_CONFIG_USERCONFIG` / `~/.npmrc`). `setup-node` dropped entirely from `release-docs.yml` + `release-types.yml` (they commit to git submodules, not npm). Three iteration rounds caught environment quirks at the source: (1) git's "dubious ownership" guard fires in container runs where the repo dir is owned by a different uid than the running process ŌĆö fixed by adding `git config --global --add safe.directory '*'` to the shared container-prereqs step (catches both manual `git submodule update` AND `dorny/paths-filter`'s direct git invocations); (2) the bare `gjs` package on Fedora 43 doesn't transitively pull `libsoup3` (+ its typelib), so install.mjs aborted at startup with `Typelib file for namespace 'Soup', version '3.0' not found` ŌĆö added explicitly to dnf prereqs; (3) ts-for-gir's project-level dev tools (biome, tsc) carry `#!/usr/bin/env node` shebangs and were missing in the no-Node container ŌĆö `nodejs` added to dnf prereqs. Phase F's "Node-free" goal is specifically about the `@gjsify/cli` install + run path; project-level npm-shebanged tools still need Node at runtime. ts-for-gir is now a working reference for any downstream consumer wanting to ship a GJS app with Node-free install.

- ~~**Phase F MVP: Node-free bootstrap ŌĆö `install.mjs` + `gjsify self-update` + `gjsify generate-installer`**~~Ō£ō ŌĆö Replaces the last `npm install -g @gjsify/cli` shellout in the gjsify install story. New surface: (1) `install.mjs` at the repo root (~250 LoC, stock GJS / GLib / Gio / Soup 3) ŌĆö downloads `cli.gjs.mjs` from a configurable URL (default = `github.com/gjsify/gjsify/releases/latest/download/cli.gjs.mjs`), verifies SHA-256 against a sidecar `.sha256` asset, caches into `$XDG_CACHE_HOME/gjsify/bootstrap/`, then spawns `gjs -m <bundle> install -g <target>`. Args: `--target <pkg>` (default `@gjsify/cli`), `--tag <dist-tag|version>`, `--bootstrap-url <url>`. (2) `gjsify self-update` (`commands/self-update.ts`, ~120 LoC) walks `import.meta.url` ŌåÆ own package.json to read current version, fetches `dist-tags[<tag>]` via `@gjsify/npm-registry`, re-uses `installPackages` + `linkGlobalBins`. `--check` shows diff, `--force` reinstalls identical version. (3) `gjsify generate-installer [target]` (`commands/generate-installer.ts`, ~100 LoC) scaffolds an `install.mjs` for any GJS-runnable npm package, substituting `DEFAULT_TARGET` / `DEFAULT_BIN_NAME` / `DEFAULT_BOOTSTRAP_URL`. The template is the gjsify-root `install.mjs` itself, symlinked into `cli/src/templates/install.mjs.tmpl` and inlined at build time via the static-read-inliner so there is exactly one canonical installer source. Three cross-cutting fixes were caught while getting the GJS bootstrap loop to run end-to-end against the live npm registry: (a) **`@gjsify/npm-registry` now sends `Accept-Encoding: identity`** ŌĆö Soup3's chunked-decoding input stream raised `G_IO_ERROR_PARTIAL_INPUT` mid-stream at the tail of npm CDN gzipped responses (upstream closes the TCP connection at a non-chunk boundary), masking 4 KB of payload as "Invalid response body". Identity-encoding sidesteps the entire chunked-gzip code path; bandwidth cost is negligible for ~64 KB packuments. (b) **`@gjsify/utils` `readBytesAsync` treats clean-stream-end Gio errors as EOF** (`PARTIAL_INPUT` / `CONNECTION_CLOSED` / `BROKEN_PIPE` / `CLOSED`) ŌĆö defensive layer for any non-npm Soup-backed HTTP source that may exhibit the same chunk-boundary close behaviour. (c) **`install-global` `linkGlobalBins` wraps `.gjs.mjs` / `.mjs` targets with `exec gjs -m '<bundle>'`** instead of bare-exec'ing them. Direct-exec only works when the bundle carries a `#!/usr/bin/env -S gjs -m` shebang, which published <= 0.4.x tarballs predate; the wrapped form works for any bundle. (d) **`@gjsify/cli` `build:gjs-bundle` script gained `--shebang`** so newly-published bundles ship with a GJS shebang (informational ŌĆö the wrapped launcher handles all historical tarballs). The release workflow (`.github/workflows/release.yml`) now uploads `install.mjs` + `packages/infra/cli/dist/cli.gjs.mjs` + a generated `.sha256` sidecar as GitHub-release assets via `softprops/action-gh-release@v2`, giving stable `releases/latest/download/...` URLs. New e2e suite `tests/e2e/install-script/` (2 tests, 1s run) exercises the full bootstrap chain against an in-process mock npm registry (success path + SHA-256 mismatch fast-fail) and is wired into the `test:e2e` aggregator. CI migration of the gjsify monorepo + ts-for-gir from `npm install -g @gjsify/cli` to the `curl ... install.mjs` bootstrap is the follow-up PR after the first Phase-F-enabled release ships the assets.

- ~~**BYOB Byte Streams in `@gjsify/web-streams`**~~Ō£ō ŌĆö Full WHATWG Streams BYOB surface added to the polyfill. Three new classes: `ReadableByteStreamController` (~600 LOC of spec helpers ported from `refs/deno/ext/web/06_streams.js:5887+` ŌĆö `enqueue`/`close`/`error`/`byobRequest`/`desiredSize` + `[[pendingPullIntos]]` + `[[autoAllocateChunkSize]]`), `ReadableStreamBYOBReader` (`read(view, {min?})` returning a typed view), `ReadableStreamBYOBRequest` (`view`/`respond`/`respondWithNewView`). `ReadableStream` constructor branches on `type:'bytes'` (was `RangeError`); `getReader({mode:'byob'})` returns BYOB reader (was `RangeError`); `tee()` routes byte streams to a new default-reader-based byte tee (full BYOB-aware tee deferred). Polymorphic helpers (`readableStreamCancel`, `readableStreamError`) handle BYOB read-into requests on close/error/cancel paths. Constructor preserves the originating typed-array constructor (Uint8Array ŌåÆ Uint8Array, DataView ŌåÆ DataView, Uint32Array preserves element count, etc.) via the `viewConstructor` slot in pull-into descriptors. New util helpers `transferArrayBuffer` (SM140 `ArrayBuffer.prototype.transfer()` with `slice(0)` fallback), `isDetachedBuffer`, `typedArrayConstructorByTag`, `elementSizeByTag`. New `byob.spec.ts` (38 tests): constructor + reader + request semantics, autoAllocateChunkSize wrap, error propagation, tee, releaseLock, `Symbol.toStringTag`. `register/readable` and `globals-map.mjs` extended with `ReadableStreamBYOBReader`/`ReadableStreamBYOBRequest`/`ReadableByteStreamController`/`ReadableStreamDefaultController`/`ReadableStreamDefaultReader`. **Cross-cutting CLI fix** (caught by this work): the `gjsify build --app gjs` virtual-entry wrapper in `@gjsify/rolldown-plugin-gjsify/src/app/gjs.ts` was emitting `export * from "<entry>"` for the user's input, which re-exports named bindings but does NOT execute the entry's top-level body. Test bundles that called `run({...})` at module top-level were silently stripped by rolldown's tree-shaker. Fixed by adding a sibling side-effect `import "<entry>"` AND marking the target's resolved id with `moduleSideEffects: 'no-treeshake'` via the virtual-entry plugin's `resolveId` hook ŌĆö this works around the package's `sideEffects: ["./lib/esm/register.js", ...]` whitelist that previously caused rolldown to drop the test body. 345 Node tests / 345 GJS tests, all green. Closes Open TODO "BYOB Byte Streams".

- ~~**Phase E: `gjsify pack` + `gjsify publish` (drop the last two `npm` shellouts)**~~Ō£ō ŌĆö Replaces the remaining `npm pack` + `npm publish` invocations in the gjsify toolchain with first-class commands. `gjsify pack` (`packages/infra/cli/src/commands/pack.ts`, ~280 LOC) honors `files`-allowlist + `.npmignore`/`.gitignore` with the same precedence as npm, always-includes `package.json` / `README*` / `LICENSE*` / `NOTICE*` / `main` / `bin`-entries, rewrites `workspace:^`/`~`/`*` to resolved version ranges in-memory (source untouched), and emits ustar tar via the new `createTarball()` writer in `packages/infra/tar/src/create.ts` + `gzip()` helper in `extract.ts` (Web `CompressionStream('gzip')` everywhere). `--json` output matches `npm pack --json` shape (array of `{filename, name, version, size, unpackedSize, shasum, integrity, entryCount, files}`). `gjsify publish` (`commands/publish.ts`, ~250 LOC) packs via the shared `packWorkspace()` helper, computes `_attachments` + `dist.tarball` with the **unscoped** basename (`cli-0.4.9.tgz`, not the scoped pack filename `gjsify-cli-0.4.9.tgz`), URL-encodes the package name following npm-package-arg's escapedName convention (`@${scope}%2f${name}` ŌĆö literal `@`, lowercase `%2f`), and authenticates by reading `process.env.NPM_CONFIG_USERCONFIG` first (where `actions/setup-node@v6` writes the auth-token npmrc) with `~/.npmrc` as fallback. Three sub-bugs surfaced during the v0.4.6 ŌåÆ v0.4.14 hotfix stretch were each fixed at the root: (1) wire-filename mismatch (`@gjsify/cli-0.4.6.tgz` 404'd because npm expects `cli-0.4.6.tgz` per `dist.tarball: https://registry.npmjs.org/@gjsify/cli/-/cli-0.4.5.tgz`); (2) URL-encoding mismatch (`encodeURIComponent + replace('%40','@')` produced uppercase `%2F` ŌĆö npm rejects); (3) auth lookup missed `NPM_CONFIG_USERCONFIG` and silently sent `authorization: (none)` despite the CI npmrc being present. `GJSIFY_PUBLISH_DEBUG=1` env-gated debug logging was added to surface the auth issue in v0.4.8's CI run. Root `package.json` `"npm:publish"` script switched from the `scripts/publish-workspace.mjs` wrapper (deleted) to `gjsify foreach --no-private --exclude '@girs/*' --exec -- gjsify publish --tolerate-republish --tag latest --access public`. `tests/e2e/pack.mjs` migrated from `npm pack` to `gjsify pack`. End-to-end verified against npm registry in v0.4.14: all `@gjsify/*` tarballs publish with resolved `^0.4.14` ranges (no leaked `workspace:^` strings), `@gjsify/cli@0.4.14` packument confirms resolved deps. With Phase E landed, the gjsify monorepo's release pipeline contains **zero `npm` CLI invocations** end-to-end (install ŌåÆ build ŌåÆ check ŌåÆ test ŌåÆ pack ŌåÆ publish all flow through `gjsify`).

- ~~**Phase D.8: ts-for-gir migrated to gjsify (cross-repo dogfood)**~~Ō£ō ŌĆö ts-for-gir (PR [gjsify/ts-for-gir#393](https://github.com/gjsify/ts-for-gir/pull/393)) is now Node-free at the install + run + foreach + workspace + publish layers. Bootstrap is `npm install -g @gjsify/cli@^0.4.14` + `gjsify install --immutable`; build/check/test routes through `gjsify run`/`gjsify workspace`/`gjsify foreach`. All three CI jobs (`check`, `test-units`, `build-validate`) green on the migration branch. Surfaced + fixed two gjsify-CLI gaps mid-migration: (1) **npm overrides + yarn resolutions support** in `gjsify install` (`packages/infra/cli/src/commands/install.ts::extractOverrides` + `install-backend-native.ts::resolveDeps`'s `applyOverride` predicate) ŌĆö without it, ts-for-gir's `resolutions: { "typescript@*": "~5.9.2" }` was ignored, transitive `typescript@*` devDeps resolved to `6.0.3`, and `tsc` surfaced three latent strictness errors in pre-existing generated d.ts (TS1540 / TS2416 / TS2320). Now both the npm-style flat `overrides: { name: version }` and yarn-style `resolutions: { "name@*": version }` shapes flatten into a `name ŌåÆ range` map and apply on every dependency edge during resolution (initial specs + transitive packument deps). (2) **`gjsify foreach --exec` mode** for arbitrary commands per workspace ŌĆö yarn's `workspaces foreach exec <cmd>` equivalent ŌĆö needed by ts-for-gir's publish chain to wrap `npm publish` correctly with the workspace-protocol-rewrite script. Use `--exec --` to pass flags through without yargs intercepting them. (3) **`scripts/publish-workspace.mjs` wrapper** in the gjsify monorepo that pre-rewrites `workspace:^/~/*` deps to resolved npm version ranges before invoking `npm publish` from a workspace directory ŌĆö yarn auto-rewrites the workspace protocol at publish-from-workspace time; `npm publish` from inside a workspace directory does NOT, only `npm publish --workspace=<name>` from monorepo root does. Without this, all `@gjsify/*` 0.4.1-0.4.3 tarballs shipped with `workspace:^` strings that consumers couldn't resolve. The finally-block restores `package.json` even on `process.exit` (initial bug was an exit-from-try that skipped the cleanup). (4) **`gjsify run` script-vs-file precedence fix**: bare names like `build` now prefer the package.json script lookup when present, only falling back to file mode if the target is a regular file (not a directory) ŌĆö meson/vala prebuilds populate `./build/` and the heuristic was masking the `"build"` script. (5) **Helper `findWorkspaceRoot` factored into `utils/workspace-root.ts`** and shared across `run.ts` + `workspace.ts` + `foreach.ts` ŌĆö previously only `run.ts` walked up; chained calls like `gjsify workspace @gjsify/adwaita-web build:scss` from cwd=website hit a `TypeError: can't access property "manifest", S is undefined` because `discoverWorkspaces(cwd=website)` returned []. All five gaps land in `@gjsify/cli@0.4.14`. ts-for-gir's tsconfig in `examples/gtk-3-editor` needed `"types": []` (same auto-include pattern fixed in gjsify monorepo) because gjsify install's node_modules layout exposes every parent's `@types/*` to tsc, unlike yarn's PnP. `packageExtensions` from yarn-berry (conditional-changelog + @parcel/* + @farmfe/*) are NOT replicated ŌĆö none surface as direct ts-for-gir deps in CI; revisit if a transitive flake appears.

- ~~**Phase 4 ŌĆö http2 hardening + frame coverage**~~Ō£ō ŌĆö Closes the 5-phase plan that promoted `@gjsify/http2` from Partial ŌåÆ Full. (1) **GOAWAY on `server.close()`**: `Http2NativeDispatcher._closeConnection()` submits a GOAWAY frame via `SessionBridge.submit_goaway()`, drains the output queue, half-closes the socket (`shutdown(false, true)`), then defers the final `close()` to a `GLib.idle_add()` tick so kernel-buffered bytes drain before the FIN. (2) **RST_STREAM on `stream.close(code)`**: `ServerHttp2Stream.close(code)` now calls `backend.reset(code)` on the native backend (no-op for Soup-backed streams), which routes through `SessionBridge.submit_rst_stream()`. (3) **GC pinning of active connections**: `Http2NativeDispatcher` keeps the per-connection `SessionBridge` instances in a `Set<SessionBridge>` until the connection drains, preventing SpiderMonkey from collecting the bridge while libnghttp2's C-side callbacks still reference it (validated by a 50-sequential-request stress test that ran clean ŌĆö no `BoxedBase::finalize` SIGSEGVs). (4) Defer (out-of-scope, low-impact): PRIORITY frames (RFC 9218 deprecated this in favor of CPRIORITY, niche), ALTSVC / ORIGIN (Node-API doesn't surface these), Vala HPACK inflate helpers (nghttp2 inflates internally inside the session driver). New tests in `http2-native-dispatch.gjs.spec.ts`: `long-running connection survives 50 sequential requests (GC pinning)` and `server.close() releases the listen port immediately` (the latter is a pragmatic refactor of the originally-planned wire-level GOAWAY observation ŌĆö in-process clients don't reliably see GOAWAY bytes due to TCP-FIN/socket-close timing; port-reuse + close-event firing exercise the same teardown path more robustly). GJS suite: 180 ŌåÆ 231 tests, all green; Node suite: 51, green. **`@gjsify/http2` is now feature-complete and Partial ŌåÆ Full.**

- ~~**Phase 3 ŌĆö http2 client-side native session**~~Ō£ō ŌĆö `ClientHttp2Session.connect()` gained `nativeDispatcher: 'auto' | 'force' | 'off'` (default `auto` keeps the Soup path for backwards compatibility; `force` opt-in routes through a new `Http2NativeClientDispatcher`). The native client runs over a `Gio.SocketClient.connect_to_host()` TCP socket plus `SessionBridge.new_client()` for the nghttp2 state machine. Same pollable-input-stream + lazy-attached SourceFunc pattern as the server dispatcher (Phase 1). New `packages/node/http2/src/native-client-dispatcher.ts` (~310 LOC) exposes `submitRequest`, `writeData`, response-header polling, async-iterable body, and surfaces server-pushed streams via the `push-promise-received` signal ŌåÆ emits as `'stream'` event on `ClientHttp2Session` (which Soup's high-level Session API never exposed). `ClientHttp2Stream` gained a `_nativeStreamId` + `_wireNativeBody()` path: writes route through `nativeClient.writeData()`; `_final` calls `submitRequest` with the buffered body and ends the stream; response headers + data are polled / iterated. Cross-cutting bug fix in `ClientHttp2Session.request()`: pseudo-headers (`:method`, `:scheme`, `:authority`, `:path`) are now reliably ordered BEFORE regular headers ŌĆö RFC 7540 ┬¦8.1.2.1 requires this and nghttp2 rejected mis-ordered requests with PROTOCOL_ERROR + RST_STREAM. Bug was harmless against Soup (Soup builds the HPACK frame itself) but fatal against the native server dispatcher. Two new e2e tests in `http2-native-dispatch.gjs.spec.ts`: `http2.connect(h2c) drives a request via the native client` (full POST round-trip through gjsify's own client ŌåÆ gjsify's own server) and `client receives server-pushed streams via 'stream' event` (server pushes /style.css; client `'stream'` listener iterates the pushed body). GJS suite: 174 ŌåÆ 180 tests, all green. Node suite: 102, green. With Phase 3 landed, `@gjsify/http2` is feature-complete ŌĆö h2c server, ALPN-h2 server (via Soup), PUSH_PROMISE wire delivery, h2c client + native client-side push reception ŌĆö and is promoted from Partial ŌåÆ Full in the package table.

- ~~**Phase 2 ŌĆö http2 PUSH_PROMISE wire delivery + h2c**~~Ō£ō ŌĆö `ServerHttp2Stream.pushStream()` now routes the PUSH_PROMISE frame through `SessionBridge.submit_push_promise()` when the response is backed by the native dispatcher (Phase 1). The promised stream id comes from nghttp2 itself (not a JS allocator), and the frame bytes are emitted on the wire ŌĆö `pushPromiseFrame` stays `null` on the native path; the Soup-fallback path keeps the cached-frame contract intact for backwards compatibility. `Http2NativeBackend` grew a `pushPromise(headers) ŌåÆ Http2NativeBackend | null` factory: pushed streams reuse the parent's TCP connection (single HTTP/2 session) and get a sibling backend that the pushed `Http2ServerResponse` writes through. Cross-cutting bug fix in `@gjsify/http2-native`'s C shim: `on_begin_headers_cb` / `on_header_cb` accumulator was keyed by `frame->hd.stream_id` for PUSH_PROMISE frames (which is the PARENT stream id) ŌĆö headers describing the promised resource never reached the bridge. Fixed by `accum_key_for_frame()` helper that switches to `frame->push_promise.promised_stream_id` for PUSH_PROMISE; client-side `push-promise-received` signal now surfaces complete header sets keyed by the promised id. New e2e test `delivers PUSH_PROMISE on the wire ŌĆö client sees the promised stream` in `http2-native-dispatch.gjs.spec.ts` exercises the full path: in-process SessionBridge client receives the push promise via `push-promise-received`, then both main response + pushed resource bodies arrive on the same TCP connection. 174 GJS / 102 Node tests, all green. Client-side `'push'` event delivery through `@gjsify/http2`'s `ClientHttp2Session` still routes via Soup (no push surfacing); native client-side reception lands in Phase 3.

- ~~**Phase 1 ŌĆö http2 native dispatcher on Gio.SocketService**~~Ō£ō ŌĆö `@gjsify/http2`'s `createServer({allowHTTP1: false})` now opens a `Gio.SocketService` and routes accepted sockets through a fresh `Http2NativeDispatcher` (new `packages/node/http2/src/native-dispatcher.ts`, ~330 LOC). Each connection owns its own `SessionBridge` (server mode) plus a `Gio.PollableInputStream.create_source()` watch ŌĆö `Gio.Socket.create_source()` is marked `introspectable=0` in the GIR so we can't use it directly from JS. Same for `Gio.Socket.receive()`: not callable from JS because the `buffer` out-param fails `caller-allocates` introspection. We use `InputStream.read_bytes(count, cancellable)` instead, which the pollable source guarantees won't block. `Http2ServerResponse` grew a `Http2NativeBackend` interface + `_nativeBackend` field so `_startStreaming`/`_write`/`_final` route through `SessionBridge.submit_response/submit_data` when the dispatcher is attached; Soup-backed responses keep their existing path verbatim. New option `Http2ServerOptions.nativeDispatcher?: 'auto'|'force'|'off'` (default `auto`): `allowHTTP1: false` + `auto` triggers the dispatcher; `off` rejects with a precise error. New spec `packages/node/http2/src/http2-native-dispatch.gjs.spec.ts` exercises the full h2c handshake + response round-trip end-to-end via an in-process `SessionBridge.new_client()` riding on a `Gio.SocketClient` TCP socket (avoids the curl-subprocess + node:http2-client wiring): GET response with body, POST echo with body, three concurrent streams on one connection. 166 GJS tests / 102 Node tests green (was 149 / 102) ŌĆö no regressions in Soup path. Phase 2 (PUSH_PROMISE wire delivery ŌĆö flips `@gjsify/http2` Partial ŌåÆ Full) lands in the next PR.

- ~~**Phase 0 ŌĆö http2 native session scaffold**~~Ō£ō ŌĆö `@gjsify/http2-native`'s `SessionBridge` Vala class now owns a full `nghttp2_session` (server + client) instead of just preface detection. New C shim around `nghttp2_session_{server,client}_new` / `nghttp2_session_mem_{recv,send}` + the submit family (`submit_settings/response/request/data/push_promise/goaway/rst_stream`); per-stream HEADERS accumulator + GLib.Bytes-owned DATA carrier keep buffer ownership C-side. Events drain through `gjsify_http2_event_*` getters (opaque pointer, no struct emitted by Vala) and re-emit on the GLib main loop via `GLib.Idle.add()` (same hop pattern as `@gjsify/webrtc-native`). Header signals carry `GLib.Variant("a(ss)")` instead of `string[]` so GJS's marshaller doesn't trip the `G_VALUE_HOLDS_POINTER` assertion. `FrameEncoder` grew SETTINGS / WINDOW_UPDATE / PING / RST_STREAM / GOAWAY builders alongside the existing DATA/HEADERS/PUSH_PROMISE primitives. New `tests/integration/http2-native/`-style spec at `packages/node/http2-native/src/ts/session-bridge.gjs.spec.ts` ŌĆö drives a server + client `SessionBridge` pair through preface + SETTINGS exchange, full HEADERS/DATA round-trip with body, GOAWAY notification, plus frame-builder unit assertions: 78 assertions green under `gjs 1.86`. No socket I/O involved ŌĆö Phase-0 scope. Phase-1 (Gio.SocketService dispatcher) and Phase-2 (PUSH_PROMISE wire delivery, **Partial ŌåÆ Full**) land in subsequent PRs.

- ~~**Phase D.7d: drop yarn entirely from the gjsify monorepo**~~Ō£ō ŌĆö yarn is no longer required to bootstrap, build, test, or publish the gjsify monorepo. The full install/test pipeline is `gjsify install --immutable && gjsify foreach build && gjsify foreach test`, with the gjsify CLI itself bootstrapped from the committed `packages/infra/cli/dist/cli.gjs.mjs` GJS bundle (Phase D.7b.1). Concrete deltas: (1) `.github/workflows/main.yml` swaps `yarn install --immutable` ŌåÆ `gjsify install --immutable`; the "Test WebGL conformance" step gained `PATH="$PWD/node_modules/.bin:$PATH"` so it can find the locally-installed `gjsify` bin without going through `npm exec`. (2) Repo cleanup ŌĆö `.yarnrc.yml`, `yarn.lock`, and `.yarn/releases/` removed from version control; `.gitignore` collapsed the unpins (we no longer ship a yarn release in-repo). `packageManager: "yarn@4.14.1"` removed from root `package.json`. `npm:publish` script switched from `yarn workspaces foreach ŌĆ” npm publish` to `gjsify foreach ŌĆ” npm publish`. (3) Bulk substitution `npm run` ŌåÆ `gjsify run` across all 164 workspace `package.json` files (418 replacements) so child scripts compose through the gjsify CLI. (4) Tooling that previously shelled out to yarn rewritten to walk `pkg.workspaces` directly: `tests/e2e/pack.mjs` (npm pack per workspace via inline glob expansion + `npm pack --pack-destination`), `tests/lint-engines.mjs`, `packages/infra/create-gjsify/scripts/process-template.mjs`. `tests/e2e/native-install/run.mjs` dropped its `yarn node` harness in favor of plain `node`. (5) Added explicit `"files"` arrays to 79 publishable `@gjsify/*` packages ŌĆö npm pack defaults to `.gitignore` when `files` is absent, and the root `.gitignore` excludes `lib/`, so build artifacts were silently stripped from published tarballs (surfaced by the create-app E2E `web-server-express` template scaffolding `@gjsify/events` and getting an empty package). (6) Added 9 missing `@gjsify/*` workspace dependencies to packages that referenced them transitively ŌĆö yarn's hoist masked the gap, but `gjsify install`'s strict per-workspace symlink layout requires explicit declaration. (7) Build-race fix: `gjsify foreach build -tp` excludes `@gjsify/cli` (which `build:infra` already builds sequentially) ŌĆö without the exclude, tsc rewrote the CLI's `lib/` while consumers were linking it, causing `SyntaxError: missing export` flakes on Fedora 43. (8) `gjsify run`/`workspace`/`foreach` commands gained explicit `process.exit(0)` after the `await close` to keep `ensureMainLoop` from blocking GJS process termination after success. PR #179 lands all of the above. The 4 PnP-related E2E tests (`pnp-zip-static-reads`, `cli-only-pnp`, `helpers.mjs` PnP path) still call yarn but self-skip when yarn is missing ŌĆö they exist to validate gjsify's PnP-compat surface, separate from the dogfooding migration. Both Fedora 43 and Fedora 44 runners green end-to-end.
- ~~**Phase D.7b: install backend nested-`node_modules` for version-conflict resolution**~~Ō£ō ŌĆö The flat single-version-per-name resolver couldn't install the gjsify monorepo because `replacestream@4` needs `readable-stream@2` while other deps pull in `readable-stream@3`; the flat resolver picked `@3` for both and `replacestream/index.js`'s `require('readable-stream/transform')` crashed. The resolver now mirrors npm v3+ semantics: each `(requester ŌåÆ dep ŌåÆ range)` edge is checked against the ancestor `node_modules` chain (`findVisible(requesterPath, name, byPath)`); compatible placements are reused, conflicting ones are nested under the requester's `node_modules/`. Top-level specs always hoist (root-level placement). Each `ResolvedNode` carries an `installPath` (`node_modules/<name>` or `node_modules/<parent>/node_modules/<dep>`). Lockfile schema bumped to v2: `packages` map keyed by `installPath` so both hoisted and nested entries coexist in the same JSON. Linker walks paths in depth-first order (parents extract before children to avoid race-on-`rm -rf`). `linkBins` restricted to root-level packages (depth-1 entries) ŌĆö matches the only consumer surface that gjsify hits. Optional-dep failures no longer throw ŌĆö they're skipped with a verbose-log note (matches npm/yarn). Side fix in `install.ts`: `syncLockfileRequested` rewrites `lockfile.requested` to match the post-update `package.json` specs, eliminating the spurious drift error that hit users running `gjsify install <bare-name>` followed by `gjsify install --immutable`. New e2e suite `tests/e2e/install-version-conflict/run.mjs` ŌĆö 4 tests against a synthetic `readable@2 vs @3` conflict scenario: layout (one major hoisted, the other nested), Node CJS resolver visibility (`require('readable')` from `bridge-pkg` returns major 2 while from `modern-pkg` returns major 3), lockfile v2 schema (both entries pinned with their full install paths, both majors covered), `--immutable` replay restores the tree byte-for-byte from the lockfile. Existing `native-install` + `native-install-project` e2e suites updated to read the v2 path-keyed schema. 19 install-suite e2e tests green.
- ~~**Phase D.7b.1: committed GJS-runnable CLI bundle + `gjsify.bin` field for Node-free distribution**~~Ō£ō ŌĆö `packages/infra/cli/dist/cli.gjs.mjs` (6.0 MB single-file ESM bundle, produced by `gjsify build src/index.ts --app gjs`) is now committed to the repository. Determinism verified: rebuilding twice from the same source produces byte-identical output, so a `git diff --exit-code` is a sufficient freshness check. Three things changed: (1) `packages/infra/cli/package.json` gained a `gjsify.bin` block (`{ "gjsify": "./dist/cli.gjs.mjs" }`) ŌĆö `install-global.ts:130-132` was already wired to honour this field and create a `<bin>-gjs` wrapper that invokes `gjs -m <bundle>`. The Node `bin` field stays for npm-compat. `files: ["lib", "dist/cli.gjs.mjs"]` ships both in the published tarball. (2) New `build:gjs-bundle` script in the CLI workspace; the root `build` chain composes it after `tsc` so every `yarn run build` produces a fresh bundle on the developer's machine. (3) `.github/workflows/main.yml` gained a "Verify committed CLI GJS bundle is up-to-date" step after `Build` that runs `git diff --exit-code -- packages/infra/cli/dist/cli.gjs.mjs` ŌĆö if the working-tree bundle (just refreshed by `yarn run build`) differs from what's committed, CI fails with a clear "refresh locally and commit" error. No auto-commit bot needed; the PR author refreshes the bundle and pushes the updated bytes. `.gitignore` updated to whitelist the bundle (the surrounding `dist/` rule still ignores everything else). End-to-end smoke: `gjs -m packages/infra/cli/dist/cli.gjs.mjs --version` prints `0.4.14` under stock GJS. This is the foundation for D.7b proper (CI swaps `yarn install --immutable` ŌåÆ `gjs -m cli.gjs.mjs install --immutable`); the actual swap is blocked on the install backend's nested-`node_modules` work ŌĆö see Open TODOs.
- ~~**Phase D.7a: root `package.json` scripts migrated from yarn to gjsify**~~Ō£ō ŌĆö Every root-level workspace-orchestration script now invokes `gjsify foreach ŌĆ”` / `gjsify workspace ŌĆ”` in place of `yarn workspaces foreach ŌĆ”` / `yarn workspace ŌĆ”`. Affects 11 foreach-style and 4 workspace-style scripts: `test`, `test:examples`, `test:examples:net`, `test:integration{,:node,:gjs}`, `check`, `check:examples`, `clear`, `clear:examples`, `build`, `build:examples`, `docs:{dev,build,serve}`. Two scripts intentionally stay on yarn: `build:infra` (bootstrap ŌĆö runs before the gjsify CLI is built, so its `lib/index.js` doesn't exist on a fresh checkout) and `npm:publish` (uses yarn's non-`run` shape `ŌĆ” npm publish --tag latest` which `gjsify foreach` doesn't model). CI continues to invoke scripts via `yarn install --immutable && yarn run build && ŌĆ”` ŌĆö only the *script implementations* changed, not how CI calls them; bootstrap path stays yarn so the dog-fooding is non-destructive. Fix in `foreach.ts`: the `--no-private` option was renamed from a literal `'no-private'` declaration to `private` (default `true`) so yargs's standard `--no-X` auto-negation handles it cleanly; the old literal name tripped strict-mode "unknown argument: private" when invoked from `npm run ŌĆ”`. STATUS for D.7b (drop `yarn.lock`/`.yarnrc.yml`/`.yarn/`, swap CI to `gjsify install --immutable`): blocked on bootstrap-strategy decision (commit prebuilt `cli.gjs.mjs` vs. `npm install -g @gjsify/cli` step vs. hybrid yarn-bootstrap). Tracked in Open TODOs.
- ~~**Phase D.6: `gjsify install --immutable` CI mode (lockfile byte-stability + drift error)**~~Ō£ō ŌĆö New `--immutable` flag on `gjsify install` (yarn's `--immutable` / npm's `--frozen-lockfile` equivalent) plumbs through both the single-project and workspace-aware install paths to `installPackagesNative` via the existing `frozen` field. CI-mode semantics: (1) `gjsify-lock.json` MUST exist at the install prefix ŌĆö otherwise a precise error fires (`--immutable requires gjsify-lock.json at <prefix> ŌĆö none found. Run gjsify install ŌĆ”`); (2) the lockfile's `requested[]` set MUST match the live request derived from `package.json` (after the D.1 carryover-merge logic) ŌĆö drift surfaces a diff listing of `+ added-spec` / `- removed-spec` lines naming the exact deps that changed, so CI failures point at the cause without forcing the user to JSON-diff lockfiles by hand; (3) when in sync, the lockfile is consumed verbatim ŌĆö `node_modules/` is populated from the pinned `resolved` tarball URLs + SRI integrity, but `gjsify-lock.json` itself is NEVER rewritten (the byte-stability guarantee CI depends on ŌĆö previously a stale-lockfile `frozen` path could silently bypass drift detection). New `describeLockfileDrift(lockfile, specs)` helper returns null for in-sync, otherwise a `+ added\n- removed` block. Hard-error guards reject `--immutable <pkg>` (yarn matches: "does not accept package arguments") and `--immutable --global` (no lockfile concept). New e2e suite `tests/e2e/install-immutable/run.mjs` ŌĆö 6 tests: missing-lockfile error, drift detection (with named diff in output), in-sync install + byte-equivalent lockfile post-condition (BEFORE / AFTER comparison after `rm -rf node_modules && gjsify install --immutable`), `<pkg>` rejection, `--global` rejection, workspace-root happy path (D.3 + D.6 interaction). Wired into `yarn test:e2e` aggregator + `yarn test:e2e:install-immutable`. This was the last yarn-replacement piece before the gjsify monorepo can run its own CI on `gjsify install --immutable` + `gjsify foreach` + `gjsify run` (Phase D.7).
- ~~**Phase D.5: `gjsify run` dual-mode script-runner (yarn-run replacement)**~~Ō£ō ŌĆö `gjsify run <target> [args..]` now dispatches between two modes based on a `looksLikeFile(target)` heuristic: targets with a path separator (`./`, `../`, `/`, `\`), a JS-ish extension (`.js`, `.mjs`, `.cjs`, `.gjs`), or that resolve to an existing path on disk go to the existing `runGjsBundle` path (gjs bundle execution with `LD_LIBRARY_PATH`+`GI_TYPELIB_PATH` set by `computeNativeEnvForBundle`). Everything else is treated as a script name and looked up in the current workspace's `package.json#scripts`. Script mode mirrors `yarn run` / `npm run` semantics: PATH is prepended with `<cwd>/node_modules/.bin` AND the monorepo-root `node_modules/.bin` (covers locally-installed bins and hoisted bins); execution goes through `shell: true` so `&&` / `|` / env-var refs work exactly as in package.json scripts; extra positional args are shell-escaped and appended verbatim; yarn-compat env vars (`npm_lifecycle_event`, `npm_package_name`, `npm_package_version`) are set so child scripts can introspect the running pipeline. Monorepo-root discovery walks up from cwd looking for a `package.json` with `"workspaces"`, sanity-checked via `discoverWorkspaces` so we don't pick up an unrelated grand-parent monorepo (matters for showcases nested inside the gjsify repo). Users who want to force file-mode for an unambiguous script name can pass `./<file>` explicitly. New e2e suite `tests/e2e/run-command/run.mjs` ŌĆö 9 tests: script lookup, npm_lifecycle_event/npm_package_name env, args forwarding (incl. shell-special chars), PATH augmentation (verified by calling a fake-bin via plain name from a workspace script), missing-script error message + available-scripts hint, missing-package.json error, exit-code propagation, file-mode dispatch for `./<file>` and `*.mjs` targets. Wired into `yarn test:e2e` aggregator + `yarn test:e2e:run-command`.
- ~~**Phase D.4: `gjsify foreach` + `gjsify workspace` commands (yarn-workspaces-foreach replacement)**~~Ō£ō ŌĆö New `foreach.ts` and `workspace.ts` commands wire `@gjsify/workspace`'s discovery/graph/filter helpers (Phase D.2) into a CLI surface that's a drop-in for `yarn workspaces foreach` and `yarn workspace <name>`. Flag parity: `-A/--all`, `-p/--parallel`, `-t/--topological`, `--topological-dev`, `--include <glob>` (repeatable), `--exclude <glob>` (repeatable), `--no-private`, `--verbose`, `-j/--jobs`. Three run modes: sequential (default), parallel (output line-prefixed `[<workspace-name>]`, `--jobs` defaults to CPU count), topological-parallel (workers pull from the readiness frontier, each workspace starts only after its in-set deps complete). Skips workspaces that don't declare the requested script ŌĆö matches yarn's behavior and prevents the user from having to `--exclude` half the repo. `detectPackageManager()` honors `npm_config_user_agent` so `gjsify foreach` invoked through `yarn run`/`npm run` keeps using the parent's runner; defaults to `npm` for portability. `gjsify workspace <name> <script>` is the 17-call-site shortcut from gjsify's root package.json. New e2e suite `tests/e2e/foreach-command/run.mjs` ŌĆö 8 tests against a synthetic 3-workspace monorepo: sequential, --include/--exclude, --parallel + line-prefixed stdout, --topological order (utils ŌåÆ core ŌåÆ app), failure exit-code propagation, workspace shortcut + error on missing workspace.
- ~~**Phase D.3: workspace-aware `gjsify install` (yarn-install replacement for monorepo root)**~~Ō£ō ŌĆö When `gjsify install` (no args) runs in a project whose `package.json` declares `"workspaces"`, the new `workspaceInstall(cwd)` path takes over. It discovers every workspace via `@gjsify/workspace::discoverWorkspaces`, aggregates the union of their external (non-`workspace:`) deps, runs the native install backend ONCE at the root prefix so externals land in a single `node_modules/` (poor-man's hoisting ŌĆö BFS resolver picks first-match per package name; per-workspace nested `node_modules/` for version-conflict cases tracked as D.3 follow-up), then materializes one relative symlink per `workspace:`-protocol dep so `<ws>/node_modules/<dep-name>` points at the sibling workspace dir. Lockfile (`gjsify-lock.json`) is written at the root. Re-install is idempotent: pre-existing symlinks at each link path are unlinked + recreated. Orphan `workspace:`-references (target workspace missing) surface a clear error naming the dep + the requesting workspace. Smoke-tested against a synthetic 3-workspace monorepo: external dep (`ms@^2.1`) lands in root `node_modules/ms/`, `@scope/utils` symlinked into `packages/app/node_modules/@scope/utils ŌåÆ ../../../utils`, Node's `import` resolves the symlinked package correctly. New e2e suite `tests/e2e/workspace-install/run.mjs` (4 tests: discovery + externals, symlink shape, re-install idempotency, orphan workspace error). Wired into `yarn test:e2e` aggregator + `yarn test:e2e:workspace-install`. The D.1 "refuses workspace root" guard was removed from `tests/e2e/native-install-project/run.mjs` as the case is now exercised by the new suite.
- ~~**Phase D.2: `@gjsify/workspace` package ŌĆö yarn-workspaces-compatible discovery + resolution**~~Ō£ō ŌĆö New package `packages/infra/workspace/` exposes four functions that together model the parts of yarn workspaces gjsify needs: `discoverWorkspaces(root)` reads `pkg.workspaces` (string-array or `{packages, nohoist}` shape), expands the limited glob set every monorepo actually uses (`packages/*`, `tests/integration/*`, `pkg-*`), parses each workspace's package.json into a `Workspace { location, relativeLocation, name, version, manifest, private }` record. `resolveWorkspaceProtocol(spec, name, workspaces)` translates yarn's `workspace:^` / `workspace:~` / `workspace:*` / `workspace:<range>` descriptors against the discovered set. `buildDependencyGraph(workspaces)` produces inter-workspace adjacency (registry deps excluded; default skips devDeps to match yarn's `--topological` flag ŌĆö gjsify's own devDep graph is cyclic, `--topological-dev` is the opt-in for the dev edges). `topologicalSort(graph)` runs Kahn's algorithm with deterministic sorted enqueue, throws on cycle. `filterWorkspaces(...)` honors `--include` / `--exclude` glob patterns + `--no-private`. Smoke-tested against the actual gjsify monorepo: 193 workspaces discovered, full topological sort completes, `@gjsify/cli` lands near the end of the order as expected (it depends on most of the tree). 29 unit specs in `index.spec.ts` (hermetic ŌĆö each test builds a fresh fixture under `mkdtempSync`). Cross-platform Node + GJS. Consumed by Phase D.3 (workspace install), D.4 (`gjsify foreach`), D.5 (`gjsify run` script-runner).
- ~~**Phase D.1: `gjsify install <pkg>` routes through native backend (Node-free project-local install)**~~Ō£ō ŌĆö Project-local installs (`gjsify install`, `gjsify install <pkg>`) no longer spawn `npm install` as a subprocess. They use the same `installPackagesNative` pipeline (`@gjsify/{semver,npm-registry,tar}`) that `gjsify dlx` and `gjsify install -g` were already on. Package.json is updated with the resolved `^x.y.z` range (or user-explicit range if pinned), lockfile (`gjsify-lock.json`) is written, layered `.npmrc` resolution (home + project) lands, and `npm_config_registry` env honored. Two early-fail guards: workspace-root install (`pkg.workspaces` present) surfaces a precise "Phase D.3" error pointing at the in-progress workstream rather than producing a half-broken `node_modules/` layout; Yarn-Berry PnP-project (`.pnp.cjs` present) surfaces the same shape. Legacy npm flow stays available via `GJSIFY_INSTALL_BACKEND=npm` escape-hatch. New helpers: `packages/infra/cli/src/utils/pkg-json-edit.ts` (parseSpec, addDependencyEntry, projectSpecsFromPackageJson, defaultRangeFromVersion); `installPackagesNative` now returns `InstalledTopLevel[]` so the CLI can update package.json from the resolved versions. Cumulative spec on existing-deps preservation: `gjsify install <new>` combines new spec with existing pkg.json deps so the lockfile doesn't churn. New e2e suite `tests/e2e/native-install-project/` (6 tests against an in-process mock npm registry: single-pkg + transitive deps, explicit version specs, `--save-dev`, lockfile reproducibility, workspace-root rejection, PnP fallback). Wired into `yarn test:e2e` + `yarn test:e2e:native-install-project`.
- ~~**Phase C: `createRequire` exports-map support**~~Ō£ō ŌĆö `packages/node/module/src/index.ts` now honors `pkg.exports` for both root (`.`) and subpath imports per the Node ESM Package Exports spec. Supported: shorthand string form, object form with `.` + `./<sub>` keys, conditional resolution (default order `["node", "import", "default"]` ŌĆö first matching wins), `null` block. Out-of-scope for this PR (tracked as future work): pattern wildcards (`./shims/*`), subpath imports (`#internal`), conditional `import`/`require` differentiation. New helpers `resolveExportsMap`, `pickConditionalValue`, `splitBareSpecifier`. Wired into `resolveInNodeModules` so subpath imports like `@gjsify/rolldown-plugin-gjsify/shims/console-gjs` resolve through the exports map first, falling back to literal-path walking. Cleanup: `gjs.ts::resolveConsoleShim` no longer needs its manual node_modules walker ŌĆö a single `createRequire(import.meta.url).resolve('@gjsify/.../shims/console-gjs')` call works under both Node and the bundled GJS-CLI. 2 new specs in `packages/node/module/src/index.spec.ts` (132/132 ŌåÆ 134/134). All 5 self-host e2e tests still green.
- ~~**Phase B: Flatpak `Sdk.Extension.node24` strip from default**~~Ō£ō ŌĆö `tests/e2e/flatpak/run.mjs` default fixture no longer includes `sdkExtensions: ['org.freedesktop.Sdk.Extension.node24']`; the assertion now confirms pure-gjsify projects get manifests **without** any `sdk-extensions` or `build-options` block (smaller, more correct). The `deriveAppendPath`-derivation logic stays covered by a new regression test that explicitly passes `--sdk-extension org.freedesktop.Sdk.Extension.llvm17` (projects with real native-toolchain needs still work). `packages/infra/cli/src/types/config-data.ts` JSDoc for the `sdkExtensions` config field updated to reflect the new reality (no default Node-extension). `gjsify flatpak deps` (the `flatpak-node-generator` wrapper) stays available for user projects whose own build needs Node ŌĆö only the default-inclusion changed.
- ~~**Phase A: minify byte-equivalence + STATUS doc-fix**~~Ō£ō ŌĆö Top-level `output.keepNames = true` replaces the previous `output.minify = { mangle: { keepNames: { function: true, class: true } } }` shape. The object form is rejected by `rolldown_common`'s `deserialize_minify` (`refs/rolldown/crates/rolldown_common/src/inner_bundler_options/mod.rs:311-325`) ŌĆö that custom deserializer only accepts `SimpleMinifyOptions` (Bool/String), so the GJS-CLI's JSON-deserializer surfaced "data did not match any variant of untagged enum SimpleMinifyOptions" while the Node-CLI's TS-side passed it via napi-rs without going through the buggy serde path. `BundlerOptions.keep_names: Option<bool>` is the documented top-level path that both engines honor: rolldown wires it into `mangle.keepNames.all_true()` (function+class) AND `compress.keepNames.all_true()` automatically. Result: GJS-CLI bundle for the yargs integration suite shrinks from 355ŌåÆ388 KB (now within ~12% of the Node-CLI's 439 KB; remaining delta is rolldown-internal compress-heuristic divergence not blocking us). Both bundles produce 52/52 passing yargs tests. New 5th test in `tests/e2e/self-host/run.mjs` asserts size-equivalence within 15% + semantic equivalence (both produce 52 completed). `stripUnserializable` minify-collapse removed. STATUS doc-drift on `gjsify install` reality fixed (existed but only `-g` was native; project-local is still npm-wrapped ŌĆö that's the Phase D-4 work).
- ~~**Phase D-3.4/3.6: yargs integration suite end-to-end via GJS-CLI + permanent self-host e2e suite**~~Ō£ō ŌĆö The GJS-CLI bundles the full `tests/integration/yargs/src/test.mts` fixture under `gjs -m` and the output (running again under `gjs -m`) executes all 52 yargs integration tests to green. New permanent regression suite `tests/e2e/self-host/run.mjs` (4 tests, ~17 s): bootstraps the GJS-CLI via the Node-CLI, then verifies `--version` + `--help` + simple-ESM bundle + yargs-fixture bundle all under `gjs -m` only. Wired into `yarn test:e2e` aggregator so it runs in CI on both Fedora 43 + 44. D-3.5 byte-equivalence against the Node-CLI output is deferred ŌĆö there's a known structural divergence (the native facade collapses `minify: { mangle: { keepNames: { ŌĆ” } } }` to plain `true` because `SimpleMinifyOptions` is an enum on the Rust side) which changes bundle size but not semantics; tracked in Open TODOs alongside the broader native-facade shape-normalization work.
- ~~**Phase D-3.2/3.3: gjsify CLI runs under GJS + bundles ESM projects**~~Ō£ō ŌĆö First leg of the End-to-End Self-Host Loop. `gjsify build packages/infra/cli/src/index.ts --app gjs --outfile dist/cli.gjs.mjs` now produces a 6.3 MB ES-module that runs under stock `gjs 1.88` and successfully bundles a simple ESM fixture end-to-end (`gjs -m cli.gjs.mjs build fixtures/simple/main.mjs --app gjs --outfile /tmp/out.mjs` ŌåÆ output runs and `console.log(7)` prints `7`). Five concrete blockers fixed: (1) `packages/infra/cli/src/index.ts` switched from fire-and-forget `void yargs(...).argv` to `await yargs(...).parseAsync()` ŌĆö under GJS the script ends as soon as the synchronous top-level finishes, so command handlers' async work silently exited before any I/O completed. (2) `rolldown` npm package (Rust prebuild) is no longer statically imported by `bundler-pick.ts` / `auto-globals.ts` ŌĆö its module-init code does `require('node:fs')` synchronously, which our createRequire correctly rejects under GJS. Both files now lazy-load via an indirect specifier so the GJS-CLI bundle doesn't drag in the unloadable Rust crate. (3) `auto-globals.ts::detectAutoGlobals` accepts a caller-provided `AnalysisBundler` so the iterative multi-pass detection runs through the same engine as the final build (native rolldown under GJS, npm rolldown under Node) ŌĆö wired up via the new `bundleToChunks()` helper in `bundler-pick.ts`. (4) `tryLoadNative()` resolves `@gjsify/rolldown-native` via `createRequire(import.meta.url).resolve(...)` ŌåÆ `pathToFileURL(...)` under GJS, since the SpiderMonkey ESM loader doesn't speak bare specifiers. (5) Six shape mismatches between npm-rolldown's JS API and the native facade's Rust deserializer normalized in one place: `input: string \| string[] \| record` ŌåÆ `InputItem[]`, `output: { ŌĆ” }` flattened to top-level keys, `transform.{define,inject}` lifted to top-level, `inject` map ŌåÆ tagged-enum array (`{type: 'named' \| 'default', from, imported?, alias}`), `sourcemap: false` dropped (Rust expects enum, not boolean), `minify: { mangle: { keepNames } }` collapsed to plain `true` (native facade's `SimpleMinifyOptions` is an enum). Plus: input-side shebang stripping in `inputShebangStripPlugin` so the CLI's own `#!/usr/bin/env node` line doesn't end up mid-chunk past the process-stub banner (acorn rejects `#` past byte 0); `unicorn-magic` ESM shim mirrors the upstream `node.js` entry so `toPath`/`traversePathUp`/`execFile` are reachable under `--app gjs` without enabling the `"node"` resolve condition globally; `resolveConsoleShim()` walks `node_modules` from `_shimDir` so the bundled GJS-CLI can find the `console-gjs.js` shim file. The remaining steps in the self-host loop (D-3.4 yargs fixture + plugin chain, D-3.5 byte-equivalence diff, D-3.6 permanent e2e suite) are tracked in Open TODOs.
- ~~**Phase D-3.1: gjsify CLI runtime-aware bundler default + bundler-pick test coverage**~~Ō£ō ŌĆö `shouldUseNative()` in `packages/infra/cli/src/bundler-pick.ts` now defaults based on the running runtime: under Node ŌåÆ npm rolldown (no FFI cost at install time), under GJS ŌåÆ `@gjsify/rolldown-native` (the only engine that can actually load there). `GJSIFY_BUNDLER=npm|native` still wins, so Node CI keeps using npm rolldown unchanged. Added 3 specs to `bundler-pick.spec.ts` (`shouldUseNative ŌĆö Phase D-3.1 runtime default`): GJSIFY_BUNDLER=npm forces npm even with native loadable; GJSIFY_BUNDLER=native throws when prebuild unavailable; default under Node = npm. CLI suite: 54 assertions total, all green on Node + GJS.
- ~~**Bundler migration: esbuild ŌåÆ Rolldown**~~Ō£ō ŌĆö Engine swap. CLI flag surface preserved (`gjsify build --app gjs|node|browser --globals auto`, `--define`, `--external`, `--alias`, `--shebang`, `--reflection`, `--minify`, `--library`, `--outfile`, `--outdir`, `--format`, `--log-level`, `--console-shim`, `--exclude`, `--exclude-globals`, `--verbose`). Six esbuild-plugin packages ŌåÆ 5 Rollup-shaped plugins (`@gjsify/{rolldown-plugin-gjsify, rolldown-plugin-deepkit, rolldown-plugin-pnp, vite-plugin-blueprint, vite-plugin-gettext}`) that also run under Vite for sister GJS apps. `--globals auto` retains its iterative multi-pass "after tree-shaking" detection (bundler-agnostic, load-bearing per AGENTS.md). One-release deprecation shim maps `.gjsifyrc.js#esbuild` ŌåÆ `.gjsifyrc.js#bundler`. ~46k LoC net deletion (6 plugin packages + 3 obsolete examples + `@yarnpkg/esbuild-plugin-pnp` dep + the `pnp-relay.mjs` workaround). Custom rewriter side-effects now declarative (virtual-entry wrapper for `--app gjs` console-shim + auto-globals injection; `renderChunk(order:'post')` for the GJS process stub; `transform(code, id)` for `import.meta.url` / `__dirname` / `__filename` rewrite ŌĆö independent from PnP loader, no more first-onLoad-wins folklore). Rolldown-specific deltas: CSS-as-string via `load` hook (Rolldown removed experimental CSS bundling); `inlineDynamicImports: true` for app builds; per-chunk acorn parsing in auto-globals (concatenation broke on duplicate top-level declarations); `external` accepts string|RegExp|function but **NOT glob patterns** (esbuild's `'gi://*'` / `'@girs/*'` glob entries become a `(id) => id.startsWith(...)` predicate); console shim moves from `inject` (esbuild) to `transform.inject` (Rolldown's Oxc-based equivalent ŌĆö `globalThis.console` is non-configurable on SpiderMonkey 128 so a register-style global write throws); virtual-entry `load` hook resolves the user-entry path through `this.resolve()` (string paths are bare specifiers to Rolldown, not relative paths); no top-of-bundle `createRequire` banner needed for Node ESM output (Rolldown's `__commonJSMin` + `__require` cover bundled-CJS interop, and a banner-injected `const require = ...` collides with bundled-CJS sources that declare their own ŌĆö yargs's ESM platform shim was the canary); `tsc -b --force` for `composite: true + emitDeclarationOnly: true` projects whose only imports are `gi://` URIs (TS6 plain `tsc` skips emit when every import is treated as opaque, breaking the dep chain for downstream `tsc` consumers).
- ~~**`esbuild-plugin-deepkit` reflection default**~~Ō£ō ŌĆö Changed default from `true` to `false`; opt-in per build. Prevents `function extends()` invalid-JS in TypeScript codebases with methods named `extends`.
- ~~**`esbuild-plugin-gjsify` GJS target: user inject preservation**~~Ō£ō ŌĆö Plugin now captures user-supplied `inject` arrays from `.gjsifyrc.js` and merges them alongside the console shim and auto-globals inject instead of discarding them.

- ~~**http2 Phase 1**~~Ō£ō ŌĆö `@gjsify/http2` promoted from stub to partial (128 tests: 102 Node + 26 GJS). `createServer()` (HTTP/1.1 via Soup.Server), `createSecureServer()` (HTTP/2 via ALPN+TLS), `connect()` (Soup.Session, auto-h2 over HTTPS), compat layer (`Http2ServerRequest`/`Http2ServerResponse`), session API (`'stream'` event + `ServerHttp2Stream.respond()`), `ClientHttp2Session.request()` ŌåÆ `ClientHttp2Stream` (Duplex, response body streaming), full protocol constants + settings pack/unpack.
- ~~**http2 Phase 2: pushStream + respondWithFile/FD + native bridge**~~Ō£ō ŌĆö `@gjsify/http2-native` Vala bridge (FrameEncoder backed by libnghttp2 HPACK, server-side StreamIdAllocator, h2c connection-preface SessionBridge ŌĆö all wrapped through a tiny C shim around `nghttp2_hd_deflate_*` since nghttp2 has no upstream Vala VAPI). `Http2ServerResponse.respondWithFile()` / `respondWithFD()` stream the file body through `fs.read()` 64 KiB chunks into Soup's existing chunked-write path with `statCheck()` callback honoured. `pushStream()` / `createPushResponse()` allocate even stream-ids via the bridge, build PUSH_PROMISE frame bytes via the encoder, and synthesise child `ServerHttp2Stream` instances backed by detached `Http2ServerResponse` buffers ŌĆö application code calling `pushStream(headers, cb)` gets a fully-usable stream + observable `pushPromiseFrame` for inspection; nested-push correctly rejected with `ERR_HTTP2_NESTED_PUSH`. 23 new tests (151 total: 102 Node + 49 GJS). Wire-level PUSH_PROMISE delivery + h2c server still pending ŌĆö see Open TODOs (Soup multiplexes HTTP/2 internally and refuses external frame injection; needs a parallel raw-nghttp2 server loop). - ~~**MCP TypeScript SDK integration suites**~~Ō£ō ŌĆö `tests/integration/mcp-typescript-sdk/` (108 tests) and `tests/integration/mcp-inspector-cli/` (14 tests). Surfaced and fixed: `ServerRequestSocket.destroySoon()`, `SoupMessageLifecycle` GC-guard, async-handler rejection swallowing, `McpServer` GC between requests.
- ~~**Multi-arch native prebuilds (ppc64/s390x/riscv64)**~~Ō£ō ŌĆö QEMU-based CI builds for three additional Linux architectures via `uraimo/run-on-arch-action`. `@gjsify/webgl`, `@gjsify/webrtc-native`, `@gjsify/http-soup-bridge` all ship prebuilds for linux-{x86_64,aarch64,ppc64,s390x,riscv64}. `nodeArchToLinuxArch()` in the CLI passes these through as-is.
